SELECT name, COUNT(*) AS num_citations FROM Author_list JOIN Paper USING (author_id) JOIN Citation USING (paper_id) JOIN Paper AS cited_paper USING (cited_paper_id) GROUP BY name ORDER BY num_citations DESC LIMIT 1;  
SELECT name, COUNT(*) AS num_citations FROM Author JOIN Author_list ON Author.author_id = Author_list.author_id JOIN Citation ON Author_list.paper_id = Citation.paper_id JOIN Author_list AS cited_author_list ON Citation.cited_paper_id = cited_author_list.paper_id JOIN Author AS cited_author ON cited_author_list.author_id = cited_author.author_id GROUP BY name ORDER BY num_citations DESC LIMIT 1;

SELECT Meetings.start_date_time, Meetings.end_date_time, Clients.client_details, Staff.staff_details FROM Meetings INNER JOIN Clients ON Meetings.client_id = Clients.client_id INNER JOIN Staff ON Meetings.meeting_id = Staff.meeting_id;  
SELECT m.start_date_time, m.end_date_time, c.client_details, s.staff_details FROM Meetings m JOIN Clients c ON m.client_id = c.client_id JOIN Staff s ON m.staff_id = s.staff_id;
